All the sounds in this bird soundboard are taken from live field recordings; so you get the feel of really being in a rain forest in Peru or the jungles of Africa!\r\n\r\nBenefits:\r\n\r\nFun and educational!\r\n\r\nWhether or not you love birding and bird watching, you can use this bird soundboard to identify different species of birds and distinguish between their sounds and calls.
